ex:Apple_Dessert_for_a_Crowd a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:cornflakes_crushed ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cinnamon ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "teaspoon" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:flour ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "2 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food <http://example.org/egg_yolk_plus_enough_milk_to_make_1/2_cup> ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:shortening ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:sugar ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:tart_apples_sliced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "5" ],
        [ fo:food ex:salt ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cornflakes_crushed ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:sugar ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tablespoon" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ] ;
    fo:instruction """Combine flour sugar salt and shortening. Add egg/milk mixture to flour mixture using beater. Put 1/2 of mixture into a jelly roll pan. Reserve other 1/2 for the op. Sprinkle onto dough in pan; cornflakes apples sugar and cinnamon. Cover with the other 1/2 of dough. Beat egg white until stiff spread over crust.\r
Bake at 400 degrees for about 40 minutes.\r
Glaze with powdered sugar and hot water glaze while still warm. Would also be good in a smaller pan for a coffee cake strudel breakfast roll.""" .

ex:Apple_Dumplings a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:shortening ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "3/4" ],
        [ fo:food <http://example.org/apples_peeled_cut_in_1/4> ;
            fo:quantity "6" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cinnamon ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "teaspoon" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:butter_melted ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:salt ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "teaspoon" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:baking_powder ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "teaspoons" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:nutmeg ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "teaspoon" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:milk ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:flour ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:sugar ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:water ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ] ;
    fo:instruction "Make syrup from first 5 ingredients. Make crust - roll 1/4 inch thick. CUt in 5 inch squares. Put 4 pieces of apple on each. Sprinkle with additional sugar cinnamon and nutmeg. Dot with butter. Fold corners to center; pinch together. Place 1 inch apart in greased baking dish. Pour syrup on top. Bake 375 degrees for 35 minutes. Serve warm with cream. Makes 6." .

ex:Artichoke-Mozzarella_Casserole a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:hot_pepper_liquid ],
        [ fo:food ex:olive_oil ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tablespoons" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:leaf_oregano ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "teaspoon" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:garlic_pressed ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cloves" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:green_onion_minced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:mozzarella_cheese_shredded ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "pound" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:dry_bread_crumbs ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:artichoke_hearts_drained_finely_chopped ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "ounce can" ;
            fo:quantity "14" ],
        [ fo:food ex:salt ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "teaspoon" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:eggs ;
            fo:quantity "4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:parsley_minced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tablespoon" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ] ;
    fo:instruction """Heat the olive oil in a small frying pand and saute the onion garlic parsley and oregano in it until the onions are soften well.\r
\r
Beat the eggs and stir in the sauteed mixture the artichoke hearts bread crumbs cheese and salt.\r
\r
Add a dash of hot pepper liquid and stir to mix well.\r
\r
Preheat oven to 350 degrees. Turn into a lightly greased 9-inch square baking dish and bake for about 1/2 hour or until set. Serves 4 to 6.""" .

ex:Asparagus_Stir-Fried a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:cornstarch ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:asparagus ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "pound" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:chicken_stock ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:garlic_minced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "clove" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:fresh_ginger_minced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:oil ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:soy_sauce ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsps" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ] ;
    fo:instruction "Snap asparagus at their breaking point cut diagonally into 1 inch lengths and blanch in rapidly boiling salted water. Heat a wok or skillet over moderately high heat add oil and heat until very hot. Add garlic and ginger and stir-fry for several seconds. Add asparagus and stir-fry to coat with oil and heat through. Add stock soy sauce and cornstarch and simmer for 2 to 3 minutes. Season to taste and serve." .

ex:Avocado_Chicken_Melt a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:sour_cream ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:monteray_jack_cheese_shredded ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:water ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:oil ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:ground_cumin ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cornstarch ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:egg_slightly_beaten ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:avocado_peeled_and_sliced ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cornmeal ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:chicken_breast_halves_boned_and_skinned ;
            fo:quantity "4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:red_pepper_chopped ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cherry_tomatoes ],
        [ fo:food ex:parsley_sprigs ],
        [ fo:food ex:green_onion_tops_sliced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:garlic_salt ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ] ;
    fo:instruction "Using a meat mallet and a hard surface pound the chicken to 1/4 inch thickness. Mix together the cornstarch cumin and garlic salt. Add the chicken 1 piece at a time dredging to coat. Mix the egg and water in a small bowl. Put the cornmeal in another small bowl. Dip the chicken first in the egg wash and then in the cornmeal turning to coat. Heat the oil in a large frying pan until hot. Add the chicken and cook for 2 minutes on each side. Remove the chicken to a shallow baking pan. Place avocado slices over the chicken and sprinkle cheese. Bake in a preheated 350 degree oven about 15 minutes or until a fork can be inserted with ease and the cheese is melted. Top the cheese layer with the sour cream. Sprinkle with green onion and red pepper. Garnish with cherry tomatoes and parsley." .

ex:Bake_Trout a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:margerine ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:salt_and_pepper ],
        [ fo:food ex:slices_bacon_for_each ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:flour ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:bay_leaf_crumbled ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:onion_thinly_sliced ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:fine_cracker_crumbs ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ] ;
    fo:instruction "Preheat the oven to 180˚C/Gas 4. Wash and dry the trout inside and out and season the cavity with salt and pepper and a few parsley sprigs. Wrap each fish with two rashers of bacon and secure with a cocktail stick. Lay them side by side in a shallow ovenproof dish. Bake for about 20 minutes until the bacon is crisp and the trout flesh cooked and flaky. Serve sprinkled with chopped fresh parsley." .

            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:dried_tarragon ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:garlic_minced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "clove" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:water ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:salt ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:fresh_green_beans ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "pound" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:onion_minced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ] ;
    fo:instruction "Preheat oven to 400 degrees F (200 degrees C). Pat green beans dry with paper towels if necessary; spread onto a jellyroll pan. Drizzle with olive oil and sprinkle with salt and pepper. Use your fingers to coat beans evenly with olive oil and spread them out so they don't overlap. Roast in the preheated oven until beans are slightly shriveled and have brown spots 20 to 25 minutes." .

ex:Baked_Zucchini_with_Mushrooms a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:zucchini_shredded ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "large" ;
            fo:quantity "4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:dried_oregano ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:mushrooms_rinsed ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "pound" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:pepper ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:fine_dried_bread_crumbs ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:onion ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "medium" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:eggs ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "large" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:parmasen_cheese_grated ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:chicken_broth ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:green_onion_minced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ] ;
    fo:instruction """Thinly sliced mushrooms and chop onion; combine in a 10 to 12 inch frying pan with half a cup of water. Stir often on high heat until liquid evaporates and browned bits stick to pan. To deglaze pan add 1 third cup of broth and stir browned bits free. Repeat deglazing step until onion is golden brown 2 or 3 more times using 1 third cup broth each time.\r
\r
Beat eggs to blend; stir in zucchini crumbs cheese oregano pepper and mushroom mixture. Pour into a buttered 10 by 12 inch shallow oval casserole (or a 9 by 13 inch rectangle). Bake in a 325 degree oven until set in center when shaken about 45 minutes top with green onions.""" .

ex:Banana_Cream_Pie a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:whipped_cream ],
        [ fo:food ex:bananas ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "medium" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cornstarch ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "Tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:_margarine_or_butter ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "Tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:vanilla ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:egg_yolks_beaten ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:baked_pastry_shell ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:lemon_juice_from_concentrate ],
        [ fo:food ex:sweetened_condensed_milk ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "14 oz can" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:water ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 2/3" ] ;
    fo:instruction "In a heavy saucepan dissolve cornstarch inwater; stir in sweetened condensed milk and egg yolks.  Cook and stir until thickened and bubbly.  Remove from heat; add margarine and vanilla.  Cool slightly.  Slice 2 bananas; dip in lemon juice and drain.  Arrange on bottom of prepare crust.  Pour filling over bananas; cover.  Chill 4 hours or until set.  Spread top with whipped cream.  Slice remaining bananas; dip in lemon juice drain and garnish top of pie.  Refrigerate leftovers." .

        [ fo:food ex:soy_sauce ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:green_onions ;
            fo:quantity "12" ],
        [ fo:food ex:b1less_chicken_cut_in_cubes ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "pound" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:green_peppers ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:water ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:ginger_root ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "slice" ;
            fo:quantity "1/8" ],
        [ fo:food ex:crushed_red_pepper ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:unsalted_peanuts ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:vegetable_oil ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cornstarch ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:dry_sherry ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ] ;
    fo:instruction "Mix sherry and cornstarch. Stir chicken to coat. Refirgerate 2 to 4 hours. Heat 2 tablespoons oil over high heat. Add ginger. Cook 15 seconds stirring constantly. Add pepper. Add peanuts cooked vegetables and soy sauce mixture (soy sauce water and cornstarch). Bring to rolling boil stirring constantly until thick. Serve immediately discard ginger. Serve with rice." .

            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cream_of_mushroom_soup_condensed ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "10 oz. can" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:butter_or_margarine ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "Tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food <http://example.org/zucchini_thinly_sliced_(about_3/4_lb.)> ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:garlic_minced ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cloves" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food <http://example.org/fresh_oregano_chopped_or_1/4_tsp_dried> ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:milk ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:onion_chopped ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:pine_nuts_toasted ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food <http://example.org/fresh_basil_or_1/4_tsp_dried> ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:water ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:ground_pepper_to_taste ] ;
    fo:instruction "Combine zucchini onion garlic and butter in 2 qt. microwave-safe casserole.  Cover and microwave on high setting 5 to 7 minutes stirring every 3 minutes until vegetables are tender.  Place zucchini mixture in blender container; blend until smooth.  Return to casserole dish; add all remaining ingredients except sour cream pepper and pine nuts.  Cover and microwave 5 to 6 minutes or until heated through.  Stir in sour cream and season to taste with pepper.  Ladle into soup bowls and garnish with sprinkle of pine nuts.  Serve immediately." .

ex:Crisp_Oatmeal_Fruit_Strips a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:soda ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsps" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:flour ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food <http://example.org/raisins_(or_finely_diced_prunes_or_dates)> ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:rolled_oats ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:sugar ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:egg ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:butter_or_margarine ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ] ;
    fo:instruction "Beat butter and sugar together until fluffy; beat in egg.  Stir flour with soda then stir into creamed mixture with raisins and rolled oats.  Mix well.  Divide dough into 15 equal portions.  Place 3 or 4 portions each on ungreased 12 by 15 baking sheet.  Pinch dough to shape 8 ropes and place at least 2 inches apart.  Flatten each rope into a 2 wide strip.  Bake in a 30 degree oven until golden brown about 10 minutes.  Let cool on pan about 2 minutes then cut each strip diagonally into 1 inch wide bars.  Let cookies cool on pan then transfer from pan with a wide spatula.  Store in an airtight container at room temperature up to 2 weeks.  Makes about 12 dozen." .

ex:Eggplant_Rollatini a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:marinara_sauce ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:eggplant ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "large" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:ricotta_cheese ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "3/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:pepper ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:dried_basil ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:mozzarella_or_provol1_coarsely_grated ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:egg_seperated ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "large" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:fresh_parsley_chopped ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsps" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:red_wine_vinaigrette ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ] ;
    fo:instruction """Heat broiler pan 4 inches from heat. In a small bowl beat egg slightly with a fork; stir in ricotta all but 1 tablespoon provolone 2 tablespoons parsley and pepper and mix well. Set aside.\r
\r
SLice eggplant into 12 lengthwise slices. Arrange in single layer on broiler pan; brush with vinaigrette. Broil 3 to 4 minutes until speckled with brown. Turn slices brush with vinaigrette; broil 3 to 4 minutes until brown and 10der.\r
\r
Adjust oven to 400 degrees. Spoon marinara over bottom of a 10 inch round shallow baking dish. Set aside.\r
\r
Place broiled eggplant slices on work surface. Spread each with 2 tablespoons of the filling and sprinkle with 1/4 teaspoon of basil. Roll slices; jelly roll style. Dip each in sauce in baking dish to coat. Place seam side down. Cover in marinara. Cover with foil. Bake for 35 minutes. Sprinkle with reserved mozzarella and fresh parsley.""" .

            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:pepper ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:unsalted_beef_boullion ;

            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:flank_steak ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "lb" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:minced_garlic ;

            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:linguini ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "lb" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:flour ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:butter ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:flour ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:minced_garlic ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cloves" ;
            fo:quantity "1 to 2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:chopped_parsley ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:white_wine_with_clam_juice_and_enough_half-and-half_to_make_2_cups_of_liquid ;

            fo:quantity "1/4" ],

        [ fo:food ex:chopped_clams ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cans" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:pepper ] ;
    fo:instruction "If using fresh clams open each one and cut out the flesh. Discard the shells then wash the clams under cold running water to remove all traces of sand. Add the salt to large pot of water and bring to a boil. Cook the linguini according to the directions on the package. Meanwhile heat the butter and olive oil in small saucepan. Add the garlic onion parsley oregano and pepper. Cook about 3 minutes stirring frequently. Add the wine and clams. Cover and simmer over low heat for 10 – 12 minutes. Stir in the cream heat for a minute or so then remove from heat. (Do NOT allow to boil) When the linguini is done drain and transfer to a large serving bowl. Pour the clam sauce over it and toss to coat all the pasta. Top with the parmesan cheese or serve the cheese on the side so people can add it to taste." .

ex:Maryland_Fried_Chicken a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:milk ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:all-purpose_flour ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:vegetable_oil ],
        [ fo:food ex:salt ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:pepper ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:butter ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:broiler_chicken_cut_up ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "pound" ;
            fo:quantity "3.5" ],
        [ fo:food ex:water ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ] ;
    fo:instruction """Shake chicken with flour salt and pepper in a plastic bag until thoroughly coated. Reserve 1 tablespoon of the flour mixture.\r
\r
Pour enough oil into a large deep skillet to make a half inch depth. Heat to 375 degrees on a deep-fat frying thermometer or until a cube of bread turns golden in about 6ty seconds.\r
\r
Carefully place a single layer of chicken pieces in hot oil; do not crowd pan. Cover and fry for 5 minutes. Uncover and fry until underside is a rich golden brown. Turn pieces cover and fry for 5 more minutes. Uncover and fry until golden brown. Remove from skillet and drain on paper towels. Repeat with remaining chicken. Pour off oil from skillet. Return 2 tablespoons of oil to the skillet. Add water. Return all chicken to the skillet skin side up. Cover and cook over low heat for 20 minutes or until chicken is 10der. Remove to serving platter and keep warm. Pour off fat from skillet.\r
\r
Melt butter in skillet. Sprinkle reserved 1 tablespoon seasoned flour over butter and cook for 1 minute. Add milk stirring and scrapping up brown bits. Cook stirring constantly until thickened. Spoon some of the gravy over chicken and pour remainder into a gravy boat and serve separately.""" .

ex:Orange-Poppy_Seed_Pound_Cake a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:baking_soda ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:unsifted_cake_flour ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "2 1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:salt ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:sugar ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:baking_powder ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "3/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:eggs ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "large" ;
            fo:quantity "4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:vanilla ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:unsalted_butter_softened ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:grated_orange_peel ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:powdered_sugar ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:poppy_seeds ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:fresh_orange_juice ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:fresh_orange_juice ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "2 1/2" ] ;
    fo:instruction "Preheat oven to 325 degrees.  Grease and flour a 9x5x3 inch loaf pan; tap out excess flour.  In large bowl beat together softened butter sugar vanilla and orange peel until pale and fluffy.  Beat in flour then remaining ingredients except the glaze (powdered sugar and 2 1/2 tsp. orange juice).  Mix until well blended.  Spread in prepared pan.  With handle of a wooden spoon make 1/2 inch deep score down center length of batter.  Bake 50-60 minutes until wooden pick inserted in center comes out clean.  Cool in pan on rack 30 minutes; invert onto rack; remove pan.  Cool completely.  To prepare glaze seal powdered sugar and orange juice in small zipper-style bag.  Gently massage mixture with fingers until blended and smooth.  Snip off corner of bag.  Drizzle glaze over cake.  Let stand 1 hour or until glaze is set." .

        [ fo:food ex:vanilla_wafer_crumbs ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:sugar ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "3/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:lite_cream_cheese ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "8 oz. pkgs." ;

        [ fo:food ex:eggs_separated ;

            fo:quantity "1" ],

            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:gelatin ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:milk ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:salt ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:lemon_juice ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:sugar ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ] ;
    fo:instruction "Crush flakes mix with butter and sugar.  Press 3/4 of mixture into spring for pan.  Chill.  Soften gelatin in water.  Beat egg yolks slightly; stir in salt sugar and milk. Add to gelatin mixture mixing well.  Whip cream until stiff.  Beat egg whites until stiff but not dry.  Fold cheese mixture to whipped cream.  Spread in pan over crumb mixture.  Sprinkle remaining crumbs on top.  Chill until firm." .

        [ fo:food ex:salt ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tsp" ;

            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;

\r

\r

\r

\r

ex:Spinach_Strudels a fo:Recipe ;
    fo:ingredients [ fo:food ex:phyllo_pastry_sheets ;
            fo:quantity "24" ],
        [ fo:food ex:fresh_spinach_stems_removed ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "pounds" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:unsalted_butter ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "6" ],
        [ fo:food ex:eggs_beaten ;
            fo:quantity "2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:shallots_chopped ;
            fo:quantity "24" ],
        [ fo:food ex:cream_cheese_sof10ed ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "ounces" ;
            fo:quantity "27" ],
        [ fo:food ex:gorgonzola_cheese_crumbled ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "ounces" ;
            fo:quantity "12" ],
        [ fo:food ex:parsley_sprigs ],
        [ fo:food ex:unsalted_butter_melted ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:dry_bread_crumbs ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "tbsp" ;
            fo:quantity "18" ] ;
    fo:instruction """Butter baking sheets. Steam spinach for 5 minutes. Squeeze out moisture. Melt 6 tablespoons of butter in a heavy skillet over medium heat. Add shallots cook for 3 minutes. Add spinach and cook until dry about 8 minutes. Transfer to large bowl. Mix in all cheeses. Arrange 1 phyllo sheet on kitchen towel. Brush with melted butter. Sprinkle with 1 tablespoon of crumbs top with second sheet butter and crumbs. Repeat with third butter and crumbs spread 1/6 of spinach mix down 1 long side of pastry 2 inches from edge. Fold 2 inches over filling then fold in sides. Roll up. Put seam side down on baking sheet. Repeat with remaining filling and phyllo. Cut each strudel into 4 slicescutting only 1/3 through. Brush with butter.\r
\r
Bake at 350 degrees for 15 minutes. After brushing with egg increase to 400 degrees and bake for 5 minutes more. Cut rest of the way through. Arrange on platter with parsley sprigs.""" .

            fo:imperial_quantity "tablespoons" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:ricotta_cheese ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:eggs_lightly_beaten ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "large" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ],
        [ fo:food ex:butter ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:shitake_mushrooms_chopped ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "pound" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:gorgonzola_crumbled ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:salt_and_pepper_to_taste ],
        [ fo:food ex:fresh_parmesan_grated ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cups" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:flour ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "cup" ;
            fo:quantity "1/4" ],
        [ fo:food ex:lasagna_noodles ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "pounds" ;
            fo:quantity "1" ],
        [ fo:food ex:dried_basil ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "teaspoons" ;
            fo:quantity "1 1/2" ],
        [ fo:food ex:frozen_chopped_spinach_thaw_and_squeeze_dry ;
            fo:imperial_quantity "10 oz packages" ;
            fo:quantity "3" ] ;
    fo:instruction """Cook lasagna noodles according to package intsructions; set aside. Place oil in large heavy skillet over medium heat. Add garlic and shallots; cook about 5 minutes until soft. Add mushrooms; cook until liquid is evaporated about 10 minutes. With slotted spoon transfer to a large bowl and reserve.\r
\r
Melt butter in skillet; blen in flour and cook for 2 minutes sturring constantly. Gradually whisk in milk; bring to a simmer. Cook stirring until sauce thickens about 5 minutes.\r
\r
Stir in gorgonzola 1/2 up parmesan and the tomato paste. Continue cooking and stirring until the cheese is melted. Stir half the mushrooms mixture into sauce. Add salt and pepper to taste. remove from heat; reserve.\r
\r
In large mixing bowl combine spinach ricotta 3/4 cup parmesan eggs basil nutmeg salt and pepper to taste with remaining mushrooms mushroom mixture; stir to blend.\r
\r
(Both sauce and filling can be made a day in advance covered tightly and refrigerated; reheat before assembling lasagna.)\r
\r
Preheat oven to 375 degrees. Spread a thin layer of sauce on bottom of 2-quart casserole or deep baking dish. Place layer of noodles over sauce. Spoon layer of spinach/mushroom filling over noodles and top with sauce. Repeat layers ending with noodles and thin layer of sauce. Sprinkle remaining 1/4 cup parmesan over top. Bake about 35 to 40 minutes or until browned and bubbly. If top browns before sauce is bubbly cover loosely with aluminum foil. Yields 6 to 8 servings.""" .
